 Ic &ae;lfric wolde &t;as lytlan boc awendan to engliscum gereorde of &d;am st&ae;fcr&ae;fte  &t;e is gehaten GRAMMATICA  sy&d;&d;an ic &d;a twa bec awende on hundeahtatigum spellum  for&d;an &d;e st&ae;fcr&ae;ft is seo c&ae;g  &d;e &d;&ae;ra boca andgit unlic&d;; and ic &t;ohte  &t;&ae;t &d;eos boc mihte fremian iungum cildum to anginne &t;&ae;s cr&ae;ftes  o&d;&d;&ae;t hi to maran andgyte becumon. 
 &AE;lcum men gebyra&d;  &t;e &ae;nigne godne cr&ae;ft h&ae;f&d;  &t;&ae;t he &d;one do nytne o&d;rum mannum and bef&ae;ste &t;&ae;t pund  &t;e him god bef&ae;ste  sumum o&d;rum men  &t;&ae;t godes feoh ne &ae;tlicge and he beo ly&d;re &t;eowa gehaten and beo gebunden and geworpen into &d;eostrum  swaswa &t;&ae;t halige godspel seg&d;. 
 Iungum mannum gedafena&d;  &t;&ae;t hi leornion sumne wisdom and &d;am ealdum gedafena&d;  &t;&ae;t hi t&ae;con sum gerad heora iunglingum  for&d;an &d;e &d;urh lare by&d; se geleafa gehealden. 
 And &ae;lc man  &d;e wisdom lufa&d;  by&d; ges&ae;lig  and  se &d;e na&d;or nele ne leornian ne t&ae;can  gif he m&ae;g  &t;onne acola&d; his andgyt fram &d;&ae;re halgan lare  and he gewit swa lytlum and lytlum fram gode. 
 Hwanon sceolon cuman wise lareowas on godes folce  buton hi on iugo&d;e leornion? 
 And hu m&ae;g se geleafa beon for&d;genge  gif seo lar and &d;a lareowas ateoria&d;? 
 Is nu for &d;i godes &t;eowum and mynstermannum georne to warnigenne  &t;&ae;t seo halige lar on urum dagum ne acolige o&d;&d;e ateorige  swaswa hit w&ae;s gedon on Angelcynne nu for anum feawum gearum  swa &t;&ae;t nan englisc preost ne cu&d;e dihtan o&d;&d;e asmeagean anne pistol on leden  o&d;&t;&ae;t Dunstan arcebisceop and A&d;elwold bisceop eft &t;a lare on munuclifum ar&ae;rdon. 
 Ne cwe&d;e ic na for &d;i  &t;&ae;t &d;eos boc m&ae;ge micclum to lare fremian  ac heo by&d; swa &d;eah sum angyn to &ae;g&d;rum gereorde  gif heo hwam lica&d;. 
 Ic bidde nu on godes naman  gyf hwa &d;as boc awritan wylle  &t;&ae;t he hi gerihte wel be &d;&ae;re bysne; for&d;an &d;e ic nah geweald  &t;eah hi hwa to woge gebringe &t;urh lease writeras  and hit bi&d; &d;onne his pleoh  na min. 
 Micel yfel de&d; se unwritere  gyf he nele his woh gerihtan. 
 SECVNDVM DONATVM OMNIS VOX AVT ARTICVLATA EST AVT CONFVSA. 
 ARTICVLATA EST  QVAE LITTERIS CONPREHENDI POTEST; CONFVSA  QVAE SCRIBI NON POTEST; stemn is geslagen lyft gefredendlic on hlyste  swa micel swa on &d;&ae;re heorcnunge is. 
 Ic secge nu gewislicor  &t;&ae;t &ae;lc stemn by&d; geworden of &d;&ae;s mu&d;es clypunge and of &d;&ae;re lyfte cnyssunge. 
 Se mu&d; drif&d; ut &d;a clypunge  and seo lyft by&d; geslagen mid &d;&ae;re clypunge and gewyr&d; to stemne. 
 &AE;lc stemn is o&d;&d;e andgytfullic o&d;&d;e gemenged. 
 Andgytfullic stemn is  &t;e mid andgyte bi&d; geclypod  swaswa ys arma uirumque cano ic herige &t;a w&ae;pnu and &d;one wer. 
 Gemenged stemn is  &t;e bi&d; butan andgyte  swylc swa is hry&d;era gehlow and horsa hn&ae;gung  hunda gebeorc  treowa brastlung ET CETERA. 
 DE LITTERA. 
 LITTERA is st&ae;f on englisc and is se l&ae;sta d&ae;l on bocum and untod&ae;ledlic. 
 We tod&ae;la&d; &t;a boc to cwydum and sy&d;&d;an &d;a cwydas to d&ae;lum  eft &d;a d&ae;las to st&ae;fgefegum and sy&d;&d;an &t;a st&ae;fgefegu to stafum: &t;onne beo&d; &d;a stafas untod&ae;ledlice; for&d;an &d;e nan st&ae;f ne by&d; naht  gif he g&ae;&d; on twa. 
 &AE;lc st&ae;f h&ae;f&d; &t;reo &d;ing: NOMEN  FIGVRA  POTESTAS  &t;&ae;t is  nama and hiw and miht. 
 Nama  hu he gehaten by&d;: a  b  c. 
 Hiw  hu he gesceapen by&d;. 
 Miht  hw&ae;t he m&ae;ge betwux o&d;rum stafum. 
 So&d;lice on ledenspr&ae;ce synd &t;reo and twentig stafa: a  b  c  d  e  f  g  h  i  k  l  m  n  o  p  q  r  s  t  u  x  y  z. 
 Of &d;am syndon fif VOCALES  &t;&ae;t synd clypiendlice: a  e  i  o  u. 
 &D;as fif stafas &ae;teowia&d; heora naman &t;urh hi sylfe and butan &d;am stafum ne m&ae;g nan word beon awriten  and for &d;i hi synd QVINQVE VOCALES gehatene. 
 To &d;isum is genumen se grecisca y for intingan greciscra namena  and se ylca y is on engliscum gereorde swi&d;e gewunelic. 
 Ealle &d;a o&d;re stafas syndon gehatene CONSONANTES  &t;&ae;t is  samod swegende; for&d;an &d;e hi swega&t; mid &d;am fif clypiendlicum. 
 &D;onne beo&d; gyt of &t;am samod swegendum sume SEMIVOCALES  &t;&ae;t synd healfclypiende; sume syndon MVTAE  &t;&ae;t synd dumbe. 
 SEMIVOCALES syndon seofan: f  l  m  n  r  s  x. 
 &T;as syndon healfclypiende gecigede  for&d;an &d;e hi nabba&d; fulle clypunge  swaswa &d;a QUINQUE VOCALES. 
 And &t;a syx ongynna&d; of &d;am st&ae;fe e and geendia&d; on him sylfum. 
 x ana ongyn&d; of &t;am st&ae;fe i &ae;fter u&d;witena t&ae;cinge. 
 &T;a o&d;re nigon CONSONANTES synd gecwedene MVTAE  &t;&ae;t synd dumbe. 
 Hi ne synd na mid ealle dumbe  ac hi habba&d; lytle clypunge. 
 &T;a synd: b  c  d  g  h  k  p  q  t. 
 &T;as ongynna&d; of him sylfum and geendia&d; of &d;am clypiendlicum stafum. 
 b  c  d  g  p  t geendia&d; on e. 
 h and k geendia&d; on a &ae;fter rihte. 
 q geenda&d; on u. 
 z eac  se grecisca st&ae;f  geenda&d; on a. 
 Se st&ae;f is genumen of Grecum to ledenspr&ae;ce for greciscum wordum. 
 i and u beo&d; awende to CONSONANTES  gif hi beo&d; tog&ae;dere gesette o&d;&d;e mid o&d;rum swegendlicum. 
 Gyf &d;u cwyst nu iudex  &t;onne by&d; se i CONSONANS. 
 Gif &d;u cwest uir  &t;onne bi&d; se u CONSONANS. 
 ianua  her is se i CONSONANS. 
 uatis  her is se u consonans. 
 &D;as twegen stafas habba&d; maran mihte  &t;onne we her secgan wylla&d;. 
 Eac we mihton be eallum &t;am o&d;rum stafum menigfealdlice sprecan  gif hit on englisc gedafenlic w&ae;re. 
 de sillaba. 
 SYLLABA is st&ae;fgefeg on anre or&d;unge geendod. 
 a domo fram huse: her is se a for anum st&ae;fgefege. 
 ab homine fram &d;am menn: her is se ab an st&ae;fgefeg. 
 Hwilon by&d; &t;&ae;t st&ae;fgefeg on anum st&ae;fe  hwilon on twam  swaswa we &ae;r s&ae;don; hwilon on &t;rim stafum: arx wighus; hwilon on feowor: pars d&ae;l; hwilon on fif: stans standende; hwilon on syx: stirps stybb o&d;&d;e m&ae;g&d;. 
 de diptongis. 
 DYPTONGVS is twyfeald sweg o&d;&d;e twyfeald st&ae;fgefeg  and &d;ara synd feowor: an on ae: musae  poetae; on &t;isum namum synd &d;a twegen stafas a and e to anre dyptongon getealde. 
 O&d;er dyptongon ys au: aurum gold; &t;ridda eu: eurus su&d;easterne wind; feor&d;a ys oe: poena wite  foenum g&ae;rs o&d;&d;e streow. 
 Ne sprece we her na mare be &d;isum. 
 praefatio de partibvs orationis. 
 PARTES ORATIONIS SVNT OCTO eahta d&ae;las synd ledenspr&ae;ce: NOMEN  PRONOMEN  VERBVM  ADVERBIVM  PARTICIPIVM  CONIVNCTIO  PRAEPOSITIO  INTERIECTIO. 
 NOMEN is nama  mid &d;am we nemna&d; ealle &d;ing &ae;g&d;er ge synderlice ge gem&ae;nelice. 
 Synderlice be agenum naman: Eadgarus  A&d;elwoldus; gem&ae;nelice: rex cyning  episcopus bisceop. 
 pronomen is &d;&ae;s naman speliend  se spela&d; &t;one naman  &t;&ae;t &d;u ne &d;urfe tuwa hine nemnan. 
 Gif &d;u cwest nu: hwa l&ae;rde &d;e? 
 &T;onne cwe&d;e ic: Dunstan. 
 Hwa hadode &d;e? 
 He me hadode: &t;onne stent se he on his naman stede and spela&d; hine. 
 Eft  gif &d;u axast: quis hoc fecit? 
 Hwa dyde &d;is? 
 &T;onne cwest &d;u: ego hoc feci ic dyde &d;is: &t;onne stent se ic on &d;ines naman stede; tu &d;u; ille se. 
 VERBUM is word  and word getacna&d; weorc o&d;&d;e &d;rowunge o&d;&d;e ge&t;afunge. 
 Weorc by&d;  &t;onne &d;u cwest: aro ic erige; uerbero ic swinge. 
 &T;rowung by&d;  &t;onne &d;u cwyst: uerberor ic eom beswungen; ligor ic eom gebunden. 
 Ge&d;afung by&t;  &d;onne &d;u cwyst: amor ic eom gelufod; doceor ic eom gel&ae;red. 
 ADVERBIVM is wordes gefera  for&d;an &d;e he n&ae;f&d; nane fulfremednysse  buton he mid &d;am worde beo. 
 Word gefyl&d; his agene getacnunge mid fullum andgyte. 
 &T;onne &d;u cwyst: scribo ic write  &t;onne by&d; &d;&ae;r full andgyt. 
 adverbivm is bene wel. 
 Her nys na ful andgyt  buton &d;u cwe&d;e word &d;ar to: bene scribo wel ic write; bene scribis wel &d;u writst; bene scribit wel he writ; et plvraliter and menigfealdlice: male legimus yfele we r&ae;da&d;; melius legitis bet ge r&ae;da&d;; optime legunt selost hi r&ae;da&d;: et cetera. 
 participivm ys d&ae;l nimend. 
 He nym&d; anne d&ae;l of naman and o&d;erne of worde. 
 Of naman he nym&d; casvs  &t;&ae;t is  declinunge  and of worde he nym&d; tide and getacnunge. 
 Of him bam he nym&d; getel and hiw. 
 amans lufiende cym&d; of &d;am worde amo ic lufige: &t;onne nym&d; he of &d;am naman him ealle &d;a syx casva: nominativvm  genitivvm  dativvm  accvssativvm  vocativvm  ablativvm: et plvraliter and menigfealdlice. 
 &D;es participivm is &d;reora cynna: hic amans uir &t;es lufienda wer; haec amans femina &t;is lufiende wif; hoc amans mancipium &t;es lufienda &t;eowa man; et cetera. 
 conivnctio is ge&d;eodnys o&d;&d;e feging. 
 &T;es d&ae;l ne m&ae;g naht &t;urh hine sylfne  ac he gefeg&d; tog&ae;dere &ae;g&d;er ge naman ge word. 
 Gif &d;u befrinst: quis equitat in ciuitatem? 
 Hwa rit into &d;am port? 
 &D;onne cwe&d; he: rex et episcopus se cyningc and se bisceop. 
 Se et  &t;&ae;t is  and  &amp;  is conivnctio: ego et tu ic and &d;u. 
 Word he gefeg&d; &t;us: stat et loquitur he stent and spryc&d;; et cetera. 
 praepositio is foresetnyss. 
 Se by&d; ge&d;eod naman and worde and stent &ae;fre on foreweardan. 
 ab illo homina fram &d;am men: her is se ab praepositio. 
 apud regem sum ic eom mid &d;am cyninge: her is se apud praepositio. 
 ad regem equito ic ride to cyninge  et cetera. 
 interiectio is betwuxaworpennyss. 
 Se d&ae;l by&d; betwux o&d;rum wordum and geswutela&d; &t;&ae;s modes styrunge. 
 heu geswutela&d; modes sarnysse: heu mihi wamme. 
 pape geswutela&d; wundrunge  atat geswutela&d; ogan  racha geswutela&d; &ae;bylignysse  et cetera. 
 Witodlice on &d;isum eahta d&ae;lum is eal ledenspr&ae;c belocen  and &d;&ae;t englisc ge&d;w&ae;rl&ae;c&d; to eallum &d;am d&ae;lum  swaswa we nu sceortlice trahtnodon. 
 On &d;isum eahta d&ae;lum synd &d;a m&ae;stan and &d;a mihtigostan NOMEN ET VERBVM  &t;&ae;t is  nama and word. 
 Mid &d;am naman we nemna&d; ealle &d;ing and mid &d;am worde we spreca&d; be eallum &d;ingum. 
 Sume naman synd PRIMITIVA  &t;&ae;t synd frumcennede o&d;&d;e fyrmyste  swaswa ys scola on englisc scol  mons dun  ciuitas ceaster. 
 Sume synd DIRIVATIVA  &t;&ae;t synd  &d;a &d;e cuma&d; of o&d;rum namum: scolasticus se &d;e on scole ys  montanus dunlendisc  ciuis ceastergewara. 
 Sume synd agene naman  swaswa is Eadgar  Dunstan; sume gem&ae;nelice: cyning  bisceop  homo man. 
 Sume synd INCORPORALIA  &t;&ae;t is  unlichamlice  swaswa is angelus engel  Michael  Gabriel  Raphael. 
 Sume synd OMONIMA  ID SVNT VNIVOCA  &d;a getacnia&d; ma &t;inga mid anre clypunge: acies egc o&d;&d;e se ord on here o&d;&d;e scearp gesih&d;; aries by&d; ram betwux sceapum and ram to wealgeweorce and aries ys an &d;ara twelf tacna.

 &T;onne &d;u cwest sunu  &t;onne by&d; se f&ae;der &t;&ae;r to understanden and se hlaford to &t;am &d;eowan.

 Of o&d;rum antimbre ferrum isen  ferreus isen; aurum gold  aureus gylden; argentum seolfor  argenteus sylfren; stagnum tin  stagneus tinen; aes br&ae;s o&d;&d;e ar  aeneus br&ae;sen o&t;&t;e &ae;ren; plumbum lead  plumbeus leaden; uitrum gl&ae;s  uitreus gl&ae;sen; lapis stan  lapideus st&ae;nen; lignum treow  ligneus treowen; et cetera. 
 Sume hi synd COMPARATIVA  &t;&ae;t synd wi&d;metenlice  &t;a geswutelia&d; maran o&d;&d;e beteran: maior mare  melior betere.

 bonus god  melior betere  optimus selost; malus yfel  peior wyrse  pessimus ealra wyrst; magnus mycel  maior mare  maximus m&ae;st; paruus lytel  minor l&ae;sse  minimus l&ae;st; facilis ea&d;elic  facilior ea&d;re  facillimus ealra ea&d;ost; difficilis earfo&d;e  difficilior earfo&d;re  difficillimus ealra earfo&d;ust; gracilis sm&ae;l  gracilior sm&ae;lre  gracillimus ealra sm&ae;lst; humilis eadmod  humilior eadmodre; humillimus ealra eadmodust; similis gelic  similior gelicre  simillimus ealra gelicost; ealswa dissimilis ungelic; agilis hr&ae;d o&d;&d;e gl&ae;d  agilior hr&ae;ddre  agillimus ealra hradost. 
 Of eallum &d;isum st&ae;pum cuma&d; ADVERBIA: bene wel  melius bet  optime selost he de&d;; facile ea&d;elice  facilius ea&d;elicor  facillime ealra ea&d;elicost he de&d;; ET CETERA. 
 Sume naman synd DIMINVTIVA  &t;&ae;t synd waniendlice  &t;a geswutelia&d; wanunge  na wi&d;metennysse: rex cyning  regulus lytel cyning o&d;&d;e undercyning; frater bro&d;or  fraterculus lytel bro&d;or; puer cild  puerulus lytel cild; pater f&ae;der  paterculus lytel f&ae;der; mater modor  matercula lytel modor; mulier wif  muliercula lytel wif; soror swustor  sororcula lytel swustor; opus weorc  opusculum lytel weorc; corpus lichama  corpusculum lytel lichama; ager &ae;cer  agellus lytel &ae;cer; liber boc  libellus lytel boc; homo mann  homunculus lytel man and omuncio ET CETERA. 
 Gyt &d;&ae;r is an hiw DENOMINATIVVM geciged. 
 DENOMINATIVVM is gecweden eal  &t;&ae;t of naman cym&d;  and of &d;am hiwe synd belocene PATRONOMICA and POSSESSIVA and COMPARATIVA and SVPERLATIVA and DIMINVTIVA and manega o&d;re naman toeacan &d;isum. 
 bonus ys nama  &t;onne by&d; of &d;am bonitas godnys DENOMINATIVVM of &d;am naman. 
 Eft iustus rihtwis  iustitia rihtwisnys; socius gefera  societas geferr&ae;den; frater bro&d;or  fraternitas bro&d;orr&ae;den; uetus eald  uetustas ealdnys; castus cl&ae;ne  castitas cl&ae;nnys; sanctus halig  sanctitas halignys; uir wer  uirilis werlic; mulier wif  muliebris wiflic; puer cild  puerilis cildlic; puella m&ae;den  puellaris m&ae;denlic; uirgo m&ae;den  uirginalis m&ae;denlic; caelum heofen  caelestis heofonlic; terra eor&d;e  terrestris eor&d;lic. 
 Witodlice ealle &d;a naman  &t;e of o&d;rum namum cuma&d;  ealle hi synd DENOMINATIVA gecwedene  and &d;ara ys fornean ungerim. 
 DE GENERIBVS. 
 &AE;fter gecynde syndon twa cyn on namum  MASCVLINVM and FEMININVM  &t;&ae;t is  werlic and wiflic. 
 Werlic cyn by&d; hic uir &t;es wer  wiflic haec femina &t;is wif. 
 &T;as twa cyn synd gecyndelice on mannum and on nytenum. 
 Nu ys gecweden &ae;fter cr&ae;fte gem&ae;ne cyn  &t;&ae;t is  &ae;g&d;er ge werlic ge wiflic: hic et haec diues &d;es and &t;eos welega: &ae;g&d;er by&d; welig ge wer ge wif; hic et haec heres &t;es and &t;eos yrfenuma; ET CETERA. 
 NEVTRVM is na&d;or cynn  ne werlices ne wiflices  on cr&ae;ftspr&ae;ce  ac hit by&d; swa&d;eah oft on andgyte  swaswa ys hoc mancipium &d;es weal  hoc animal &t;is nyten: &ae;lc nyten by&d; o&d;&d;e he o&d;&d;e heo. 
 Ac swa &d;eah &d;is cyn gebyra&d; oftost to na&d;rum cynne  swaswa ys hoc uerbum &t;is word  hoc lumen &t;is leoht. 
 Ys eac to witenne  &t;&ae;t hi beo&d; oft o&d;res cynnes on leden and o&d;res cynnes on englisc. 
 We cwe&d;a&d; on ledyn hic liber and on englisc &t;eos boc; eft on leden haec mulier and on englisc &d;is wif  na &d;eos; eft on leden hoc iudicium and on englisc &d;es dom  na &d;is. 
 COMMVNE ys gyt an cynn TRIVM GENERVM  &t;&ae;t is  gem&ae;nelice &t;reora cynna: hic et haec et hoc sapiens &t;es and &d;eos and &d;is wise  hic sapiens rex &t;es wisa cyning  haec sapiens regina &t;eos wise cwen  hoc sapiens mancipium &t;es wisa weal. 
 Ealswa hic et haec et hoc felix &t;es and &d;eos and &t;is ges&ae;lige ET CETERA. 
 Cpb Sum cyn is gecweden EPICENA  &t;&ae;t is on leden PROMISCVA and on englisc gemenged: hic coruus &d;es hremn  swa hw&ae;&d;er swa hit by&d;  swa he  swa heo; hic miluus &d;es glida  &ae;g&d;er ge he ge heo; haec aquila &d;es earn  &ae;g&d;er ge he ge heo. 
 Ealswa mustela wesle ET CETERA. 
 Sume synd gecwedene DVBII GENERIS  &t;&ae;t is  twylices cynnes. 
 Hi beo&d; gemette on bocum hwilon &ae;fter werlicum cynne  hwilon &ae;fter wiflicum: hic finis &t;es ende and eft haec finis; hic silex &t;es flint and eft haec silex; hic margo &d;es ofer and eft haec margo; ET CETERA. 
 Sume synd MOBILIA  &t;&ae;t synd awendendlice  for&d;an &d;e hi beo&d; awende fram cynne to cynne: hic sanctus &d;es halga  haec sancta &t;eos halige  hoc sanctum &d;is halige; ealswa iustus rihtwis  iusta  iustum; bonus god  bona  bonum; ET CETERA. 
 filius sunu  filia dohtor. 
 Sume synd MOBILIA  &t;&ae;t synd awendendlice  on gecynde and on getacnunge  na on stemne: hic pater &t;es f&ae;der  haec mater &d;eos modor; frater bro&d;or  soror swustor; patruus f&ae;dera  amita fa&d;u; auunculus eam  matertera moddrie. 
 Oftost on treowcynne beo&d; &d;a treowa getealde FEMININI GENERIS and se w&ae;stm NEVTRI GENERIS: haec pirus &t;eos pyrige  hoc pirum seo peru; haec malus &d;eos apuldre  hoc malum se &ae;ppel; haec prunus &d;is plumtreow  hoc prunum seo plyme. 
 Ac hit ne bi&d; swa &d;eah swa be eallum treowum: haec buxus &t;is boxtreow  hoc buxum forcorfen box. 
 INCIPIVNT QVINQVE DECLINATIONES NOMINVM. 
 OMNIA NOMINA QVIBVS LATINA VTITVR ELOQVENTIA  QVINQVE DECLINATIONIBVS INFLECTVNTVR ealle naman  &d;&ae;ra &d;e ledenspr&ae;c bric&d;  beo&d; gebigede on fif declinungum. 
 Seo forme DECLINATIO  &t;&ae;t is  seo forme declinung  maca&d; hire GENITIVVM on ae: huius poetae &t;ises sceopes. 
 Seo o&d;er DECLINATIO geenda&d; hire GENITIVVM on langne i: huius episcopi &t;ises bisceopes. 
 Seo &d;ridde DECLINATIO awent hire GENITIVVM on scortne is: huius regis &t;ises cyninges. 
 Seo feor&d;e DECLINATIO maca&d; hire GENITIVVM on langne us: huius exercitus &t;ises heres. 
 Seo fifte DECLINATIO gebig&d; hire GENITIVVM on e and on i tod&ae;ledlice: huius rei &t;ises &d;inges. 
 We fo&d; nu gewislicor on &d;a forman declinunge. 
 NOMINATIVO hic citharista &d;es hearpere  GENITIVO huius citharistae &t;ises hearperes  DATIVO huic citharistae &t;isum hearpere  ACCVSSATIVO hunc citharistam &t;isne hearpere  VOCATIVO o citharista eala &d;u hearpere  ABLATIVO ab hoc citharista fram &d;isum hearpere; ET PLVRALITER and menigfealdlice NOMINATIVO hi citharistae &t;as hearperas  GENITIVO horum citharistarum &d;issera hearpera  DATIVO his citharistis &d;isum hearperum  ACCVSSATIVO hos citharistas &t;as hearperas  VOCATIVO o citharistae eala ge hearperas  ABLATIVO ab his citharistis fram &d;isum hearperum. 
 NOMINATIVVS ys nemniendlic: mid &d;am CASV we nemna&d; ealle &d;ing  swylce &d;u cwe&d;e: hic homo equitat &t;es man rit. 
 GENITIVVS is gestrynendlic o&d;&d;e geagniendlic: mid &t;am CASV by&d; geswutelod &ae;lces &d;inges gestreon o&t;&t;e &ae;hta: huius hominis filius &t;ises mannes sunu VEL huius hominis equus o&d;&d;e &d;ises mannes hors. 
 DATIVVS ys forgyfendlic: mid &d;am CASV by&d; geswutelod &ae;lces &d;inges gifu: huic homini do equum &d;isum men ic forgyfe hors. 
 quid das mihi?  hw&ae;t gyfst &d;u me? 
 unum librum do tibi ane boc ic &d;e gife. 
 ACCUSSATIVVS ys wregendlic: mid &d;am CASV by&d; geswutelod  hu men spreca&d; be &ae;lcum &t;inge: hunc hominem accuso &d;ysne man ic wrege; hunc hominem amo &t;ysne man ic lufige; hanc rem apprehendi &t;is &d;ing ic gel&ae;hte. 
 VOCATIVVS ys clypiendlic o&d;&d;e gecigendlic: mid &d;am CASV we clypia&d; to &ae;lcum &d;inge: o homo  ueni huc eala &d;u man  cum hider; o homo  loquere ad me eala &d;u man  sprec to me; o magister  doce me aliquid eala &d;u lareow  t&ae;ce me sum &d;ing. 
 ABLATIVVS ys &ae;tbredendlic: mid &d;am CASV by&d; geswutelod  swa hw&ae;t swa we &ae;tbreda&d; o&d;rum o&d;&d;e swa hw&ae;t swa we underfo&d; &ae;t o&d;rum o&d;&d;e hwanon we fara&d;: ab hoc homine pecuniam accepi fram &t;isum men ic underfeng feoh; ab hoc magistro audiui sapientiam fram &d;isum lareowe ic gehyrde wisdom; ab illa ciuitate equitaui fram &d;&ae;re byrig ic rad; a rege ueni fram cyninge ic com. 
 &T;as syx CASVS befod and beluca&d;  swa hw&ae;t swa men embe spreca&d;  gif &d;&ae;r beo&d; word to geihte. 
 Ealswa &d;u miht hi gebigean to menigfealdum getele: NOMINATIVO hi pueri discunt &t;as cild leornia&d;; GENITIVO horum puerorum doctrina &d;issera cildra lar; DATIVO his pueris ministro &t;isum cildum ic &d;enige; ACCVSSATIVO hos pueros flagello &d;as cild ic swinge; VOCATIVO o pueri  cantate bene eala ge cild  singa&d; well; ABLATIVO ab his pueris doctus sum fram &d;isum cildum ic eom gel&ae;red; ab his poetis audiui carmina fram &d;isum sceopum ic gehyrde leo&d;. 
 Seo forme DECLINATIO h&ae;f&d; TRES TERMINATIONES  &t;&ae;t synd &d;reo geendunga: a and as and es. 
 &D;a naman  &t;e geendia&d; on a  gif hi gebyria&d; to w&ae;pmanna &t;enunge  &t;onne synd hi MASCVLINI GENERIS: hic poeta &t;es sceop  huius poetae &t;ises sceopes; hic scriba &d;es bocere; leuita diacon; sophista u&d;wita; nauta re&d;ra; pirata wicing o&d;&d;e sceg&d;man; trapezeta mynetere; proreta ancerman; ET CETERA. 
 &D;a o&d;re naman  &d;e of wordum cuma&d;  synd COMMVNIS GENERIS: hic et haec agricola se &d;e &ae;cer beg&ae;&d;; hic et haec aduena &t;es and &d;eos &ae;l&d;eodige; conuiua gebeor; collega gefera; homicida manslaga; parricida m&ae;gslaga; ET CETERA. 
 &T;a o&d;re ealle  &t;e on a geendia&d; &t;issere declinunge  synd FEMININI GENERIS: haec regina &d;eos cwen  huius reginae &t;issere cwene  huic reginae &t;issere cwene  hanc reginam &t;as cwene  o regina eala &d;u cwen  ab hac regina fram &d;issere cwene; ET PLVRALITER hae reginae  harum reginarum  his reginis  has reginas  o reginae  ab his reginis. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &d;as: haec terra &t;eos eor&d;e; erba g&ae;rs; aqua w&ae;ter; pluuia ren; arena sandceosol: uia weg; semita pa&d;; silua wudu; luna mona; stella steorra; ianua geat; petra stan; unda y&d;; pagina tramet; littera st&ae;f; ancilla wyln; gallina henn; auca gos; aneta ened; columba culfre; ciconia storc; uacca cu; scroffa sugu; uita lif; olla crocca; fuscinula awul; andena brandisen and ealle naman ledenspr&ae;ce  &d;e on a geendia&d;: ealle hi syndon FEMININI GENERIS. 
 Agene naman  gif hi to w&ae;pmannum gebyria&d;  hi beo&d; &t;onne MASCVLINI GENERIS: hic Silla  hic Seneca  hic Beda. 
 Gif hi to wifmannum gebyria&d;  hi beo&d; &d;onne FEMININI GENERIS. 
 Ne bi&d; nan NEVTRI GENERIS on &d;&ae;re forman declinunge. 
 On as geendia&d; agene naman: hic Aeneas  huius Aeneae  huic Aeneae  hunc Aeneam  o Aenea  ab hoc Aenea. 
 Nis &d;&ae;r na menigfeald getel  for&d;an &d;e hit is agen nama. 
 Ealswa g&ae;&d; hic Andreas apostolus  hic Thomas  hic Matthias  hic Barnabas; ET CETERA. 
 On es geendia&d; greciscra manna naman: hic Anchises  huius Anchisae  huic Anchisae  hunc Anchisam  o Anchises  ab hoc Anchisa. 
 Nis na menigfeald getel on agenum namum. 
 Sume naman &t;issere declinunge macia&d; heora menigfealdan DATIVVM and ABLATIVVM on bus. 
 &D;a naman cuma&d; of &d;am MASCVLINVM  &t;e nabba&d; nanne NEVTRVM: haec anima &t;eos sawul  his animabus &d;isum sawlum ET ab his animabus; filia dohtor  filiabus; equa myre  equabus; asina assa  asinabus; ET CETERA  for &d;am gesceade  &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;ron gelice &t;am MASCVLINVM  &t;e hi of cuma&d;. 
 SECVNDA DECLINATIO HABET TERMINATIONES SEX: er  ir  ur  us  eus  um; seo o&d;er DECLINATIO h&ae;f&d; syx geendunga  &t;a &t;e we nu namedon. 
 &T;a naman  &t;e on er geendia&d; &t;issere declinunge  synd MASCVLINI GENERIS  beon hi agene naman  beon hi elles gem&ae;nelice  swaswa is faber smi&d;. 
 NOMINATIVO hic faber &d;es smi&d;  GENITIVO huius fabri &t;ises smi&t;es  DATIVO huic fabro &t;isum smi&d;e  ACCVSSATIVO hunc fabrum &t;ysne smi&d;  VOCATIVO o faber eala &d;u smi&t;  ABLATIVO ab hoc fabro fram &d;isum smi&d;e; ET PLVRALITER NOMINATIVO hi fabri &t;as smi&d;as  GENITIVO horum fabrorum &t;issera smi&d;a  DATIVO his fabris &t;isum smi&d;um  ACCVSATIVO hos fabros &t;as smi&d;as  VOCATIVO o fabri eala ge smi&t;as  ABLATIVO ab his fabris fram &d;isum smi&d;um. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &t;as o&d;re: fiber befor  ager &ae;cer  liber boc  culter culter  aper bar  coluber snaca  cancer crabba  auster su&d;d&ae;l  oleaster elebeam  apiaster merce  Alexander agen nama  sacer halig  niger sweart  ater blac  teter blac  dexter and dextera swi&d;ra  sinister and sinistra wynstra. 
 &T;as macia&d; heora GENITIVVM on o&d;re wisan: hic puer &d;is cild  huius pueri &t;ises cildes; socer sweor; gener a&d;um; miser earming; adulter forligr; lucifer leohtberend; signifer tacnberend; frugifer w&ae;stmb&ae;re; belliger wigbora; clauiger c&ae;gbora; corniger hornb&ae;re; armiger w&ae;pnbora; graniger cornb&ae;re; ET SIMILIA. 
 On ir geendia&d; MASCVLINI GENERIS hic uir &t;es wer  huius uiri &t;ises weres ET CETERA; hic leuir tacor; semiuir healfmann; duumuir twegra ceorla ealdor; triumuir &t;reora ceorla ealdor; quinqueuir fif ceorla ealdor; septemuir seofon ceorla ealdor; decemuir tyn manna ealdor; centumuir hundteontigra manna ealdor. 
 On &d;issere geendunge ys an nama NEVTRVM: hoc ir &d;is handbred INDECLINABILE ungebigendlic. 
 On &d;&ae;re geendunge ur ys an nama MASCVLINI GENERIS: hic satur &t;es fulla man  huius saturi  huic saturo. 
 Of &d;am by&d; FEMININVM haec satura. 
 &T;a naman  &t;e on us geendia&d;  synd MASCVLINI GENERIS: hic campus &t;es feld  huius campi &t;ises feldes ET CETERA; ortus orceard o&d;&d;e wyrtun; nidus nest; fundus wur&d;ig; ludus plega; lucus holt; fumus smic; uterus wifes inno&d;; uentus wind; cetus hw&ae;l; taurus fearr; ircus bucca; porcus swyn; uitulus cealf; ceruus heort; hinnulus hindcealf; haedus ticcen; agnus lamb; equus hors; pullus fola o&d;&d;e brid; camelus olfend; mulus mul; asinus VEL asina assa; chorus chor; populus folc and eft populus byrc; infernus hell; miluus glida; gallus cocc; coruus hremn. 
 Of &d;isum synd NEVTRI GENERIS hoc pelagus &t;eos wids&ae;  huius pelagi; hoc uulgus &t;is ceorlfolc VEL hic uulgus; hoc uirus &t;is wyrms INDECLINABILE; hoc pus &d;eos forrotednyss INDECLINABILE. 
 &T;a o&d;re naman &t;issere geendunge synd ADIECTIVA  &t;&ae;t synd togeicendlice  and macia&d; MASCVLINVM on us and FEMININVM on a and NEVTRVM on um: hic bonus homo &d;es goda man  haec bona mulier &t;is gode wif  hoc bonum uerbum &t;is gode word. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &t;as: malus yfel  iustus rihtwis  iniustus unrihtwis  magnus mycel  paruus lytel  longus lang  modicus gehw&ae;de  sanctus halig  almus halig  clarus beorht  egregius &ae;&d;ele  doctus gel&ae;red ET OMNIA ISTIVS MODI and ealle &t;us gerade. 
 Eac swylce agene naman: Martinus  Benedictus  Augustinus ET CETERA. 
 Ealle o&d;re naman &t;issere geendunge synd FEMININI GENERIS: haec Tirus anre burge nama; haec Ciprus o&d;er burh. 
 Treowa naman: haec cedrus &d;es cederbeam; fagus boctreow; fraxinus &ae;sc; liburnus &ae;sc; pirus pyrige; ET CETERA. 
 Syndon eac sume naman  &t;e synd &ae;g&d;er ge &d;issere declinunge ge &d;&ae;re feor&d;an: haec quercus &t;eos ac; laurus laurbeam; pinus pintreow; ficus fictreow; haec domus &t;is hus; colus dist&ae;f. 
 Gyt ane feawa naman &t;issere declinunge synd FEMININI GENERIS: haec abyssus &t;eos niwelnys; huius abyssi  huic abysso  hanc abyssum  o abysse  ab hac abysso; ET PLVRALITER hae abyssi  harum abyssorum  his abyssis  has abyssos  o abyssi  ab his abyssis. 
 Ealswa g&ae;&d; haec sinodus &t;is witena gemot  huius sinodi; humus molde; heremus westen; herebus hell; aluus inno&d;; fusus spinl. 
 &T;a naman  &t;e geendia&d; on eus  synd agene naman and grecisce ealle m&ae;st; hic Titheus  huius Tithei; Pentheus  Penthei; Matheus se godspellere  Mathei  VOCATIVO o Mathee ET CETERA. 
 &T;a naman  &t;e geendia&d; on um  synd NEVTRI GENERIS: hoc templum &d;is templ; hoc uerbum &t;is word  huius uerbi &t;ises wordes  huic uerbo &t;isum worde  hoc uerbum &d;is word  o uerbum eala &d;u word  ab hoc uerbo fram &t;isum worde; ET PLVRALITER haec uerba &t;as word  horum uerborum &t;issera worda  his uerbis &d;isum wordum  haec uerba &t;as word  o uerba eala ge word  ab his uerbis fram &d;isum wordum. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &d;as naman: hoc fundamentum &t;es grundweal  tectum hrof  ouum &ae;g  pomum &ae;ppel  regnum rice  telum fla  bellum gefeoht  biuium twegra wega gel&ae;te  triuium &t;reora wega gel&ae;tu  competum fela gel&ae;tu  tugurium hulc  scabellum scamel  ostium duru  signum tacn  scutum scyld  candelabrum candelst&ae;f  indicatorium &ae;stel  triticum hw&ae;te  ordeum bere  granum corn  uinum win  oleum ele  aurum gold  argentum seolfor  auricalcum goldm&ae;stlingc  stagnum tin  plumbum lead  ferrum isen  lignum aheawen treow  otium &ae;methwil  spatium f&ae;c  interuallum lytel hwil ET CETERA. 
 Is eac to witenne  &t;&ae;t &d;eos DECLINATIO ne maca&d; na hire VOCATIVVM on eallum namum on ane wisan. 
 &D;a naman  &t;e geendia&d; on er o&d;&d;e on ir o&d;&d;e on um  &t;a macia&d; heora VOCATIVVM  swaswa heora NOMINATIVVS by&d;: o puer eala &d;u cild; o uir eala &d;u wer; o caelum eala &d;u heofen. 
 Agene naman  &t;e geendia&d; on ius  wurpa&d; aweg &t;&ae;t st&ae;fgefeg us and macia&d; heora VOCATIVVM on langne i: Virgilius  o Virgili; Laurentius  o Laurenti; Dionisius  o Dionisi; Mauricius  o Maruici. 
 Gem&ae;nelice naman macia&d; heora VOCATIVVM on scortne e: socius gefera  o socie; egregius &ae;&d;ele  o egregie; magnus mycel  o magne. 
 filius sunu maca&d; on twa wisan: o fili and o filie. 
 Eac hwilon by&d; geset NOMINATIVVS for VOCATIVVM  swaswa LVCANVS cw&ae;&d;: degener o populus eala &d;u abro&d;ene folc. 
 VIRGILIVS cw&ae;&d;: o fluuius eala &d;u flod for fluuie. 
 &T;us by&d; eac on ma stowum. 
 DE TERTIA DECLINATIONE. 
 TERTIA DECLINATIO HABET TERMINATIONES SEPTVAGINTA OCTO. 
 Seo &d;ridde DECLINATIO ys mare  &t;onne ealle &d;a o&d;re  and heo h&ae;f&d; eahta and hundseofontig geendunga o&d;&d;e ma. 
 Seo forme geendung is on scortne a. 
 On &d;&ae;re geendia&d; grecisce naman and nevtri generis: nominativo hoc poema &d;es leo&d;cr&ae;ft  genitivo huius poematis &d;ises leo&d;cr&ae;ftes  dativo huic poemati &d;isum leo&d;cr&ae;fte  accvsativo hoc poema &t;isne leo&d;cr&ae;ft  vocativo o poema eala &d;u leo&d;cr&ae;ft  ablativo ab hoc poemate fram &d;isum leo&d;cr&ae;fte; et plvraliter nominativo haec poemata &d;as leo&d;cr&ae;ftas  genitivo horum poematum &d;issera leo&d;cr&ae;fta  dativo his poematibus &d;isum leo&d;cr&ae;ftum  accvsativo haec poemata &d;as leo&d;cr&ae;ftas  vocativo o poemata eala ge leo&d;cr&ae;ftas  ablativo ab his poematibus fram &d;isum leo&d;cr&ae;ftum. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &d;as naman: hoc cauma swolo&d;  thema antimber  scema hiw  onoma nama  malagma cli&d;a  agalma anlicness  aenigma r&ae;dels  plasma gesceaft  baptisma fulluht  dogma lar  scisma geflit et his similia and &t;isum gelice. 
 Seo o&d;er geendung is on scortne e  and &d;a naman  &t;e on &d;&ae;re geendia&d;  synd ealle nevtri generis: hoc sedile &t;es hleda  huius sedilis  huic sedili  hoc sedile  o sedile  ab hoc sedili; et plvraliter haec sedilia  horum sedilium  his sedilibus et cetera. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &d;as: hoc monile &t;es myne  cubile denn  ouile eowd  praesaepe binn  mare s&ae;. 
 And ealle hi geendia&t; ablativvm on i  buton gausape beodcla&d;  ab hoc gausape  and rete nett  ab hoc rete. 
 Seo &d;ridde geendung ys on scortne o. 
 On &d;&ae;re geendia&d; manega naman: agene naman werlices cynnes: hic Cato  huius Catonis; hic Milo et cetera.

 Sume synd COMMVNIS GENERIS: hic et haec ciuis &t;es and &d;eos ceastergewara  huius ciuis; hic et haec hostis &t;es and &t;eos feond  huius hostis; aedilis ys MASCVLINI GENERIS  &t;&ae;t is botlwerd o&d;&d;e byrigman. 
 &T;as o&d;re synd TRIVM GENERVM  &t;&ae;t is &d;reora cynna: hic et haec fortis et hoc forte  &t;&ae;t is strang  huius fortis  huic forti  hunc et hanc fortem et hoc forte  o fortis et o forte  ab hoc et ab hac et ab hoc forti; ET PLVRALITER hi et hae fortes et haec fortia  horum et harum et horum fortium  his fortibus ET CETERA. 
 Ealswa ga&d; &d;as: hic et haec dulcis et hoc dulce &t;&ae;t is werod; suauis softe o&d;&d;e wynsum  omnis &ae;lc and ealle DENOMINATIVA  &t;&ae;t synd  &d;a &d;e of o&d;rum namum cuma&d;: memoria ys gemynd  &t;onne by&d; of &d;am memorialis gemyndelic; uitalis liflic  pluuialis renlic  fluuialis flodlic  iudicialis domlic  corporalis lichamlic  spiritalis gastlic  hospitalis cumli&d;e  mortalis deadlic  principalis ealdorlic  fidelis getreowfull  crudelis w&ae;lhreow  similis gelic  senilis ealdlic  puerilis cildlic  iuuenilis iunglic  uirilis werlic  muliebris wiflic  seruilis &t;eowtlic  hostilis feondlic. 
 Sume habba&d; scortne i: amabilis lufigendlic  stabilis sta&d;olf&ae;st  uolatilis fleogendlic  natatilis swymmendlic  habilis h&ae;bbendlic  flebilis woplic  lugubris dreoriglic  utilis nytwur&d;lic and o&d;re &d;yllice  and ealle hi macia&d; ABLATIVVM on langne i. 
 &T;as o&d;re synd MASCVLINI GENERIS: hic panis &t;es hlaf  huius panis; ealswa funis rap  amnis ia  ignis fyr  piscis fisc  fascis byr&d;en  fustis sagol o&d;&d;e st&ae;f  postis post  uectis steng  axis &ae;x  mensis mona&d;  ensis swurd  anguis n&ae;ddre  unguis n&ae;gl o&d;&d;e clawu  collis beorh o&d;&d;e clud  follis bylig  orbis embehwyrft  corbis wylige o&d;&d;e windel. 
 Sume habba&d; o&d;erne GENITIVVM: hic lapis &t;es stan  huius lapidis; hic sanguis &t;is blod  huius sanguinis; pollis smedma of melwe  pollinis; cinis axan  cineris; puluis dust  pulueris; uomis scer  uomeris; pubis cniht o&d;&d;e cnihthad  puberis; inpubis beardleas. 
 Sume menn geendia&d; &d;as naman on er: hic puluer  ciner  uomer  puber ET CETERA. 
 &T;as o&d;re synd FEMININI GENERIS: haec cuspis &t;es sceft  huius cuspidis; cassis helm  cassidis is eac gecweden cassida  swaswa gracilis sm&ae;l and gracila. 
 gracilis ys &d;reora cynna: hic et haec gracilis et hoc gracile  huius gracilis; haec auis &d;es fugel  huius auis; haec clauis &d;eos c&ae;g  securis ex  bipennis twybile  pestis cwyld  uestis reaf  uallis dene  turris stypel  puppis scip o&d;&d;e steorsetl  nauis scip  classis sciphere  cutis hyd  pellis fel  messis gerip  bilis gealla. 
 &D;a &d;e synd gefegede of blode o&d;&d;e of mode  &t;a synd &t;reora cynna: hic et haec exsanguis et hoc exsangue blodleas  huius exsanguis; hic et haec exanimis et hoc exanime sawulleas  huius exanimis ET CETERA.

 amans lufigende is &ae;g&d;er ge nama ge PARTICIPIVM  amantis.

 sapiens is &ae;g&d;er ge nama ge PARTICIPIVM  and insipiens unsnotor of &d;am gefeged is &ae;fre nama.

 Swa g&ae;&d; istiusmodi swa gerad and eiusmodi to &ae;lcum cynne and to &ae;lcum case.

 &T;as and &d;yllice synd INDECLINABILIA  &t;&ae;t synd undecliniendlice. 
 Ys eac to witenne  &t;&ae;t ledene lareowas macia&d; on sumum namum ACCVSSATIVVM on im: haec uis &t;eos miht  hanc uim; haec tussis &d;es hwosta  hanc tussim; haec Caribdis an stanclud on s&ae;  hanc Caribdim; haec syrtis &t;es sandhricg  hanc syrtim; Tiberis hatte seo ea  &t;e yrn&d; be Rome  hanc Tiberim; Tigris ys an ea and anes cynnes deor  hanc Tigrim.
