 &T;as geendia&d; on em: item eft  tandem &ae;t nextan  ibidem &t;ar rihte  identidem efsona. 
 &D;as geendia&d; on im: pars d&ae;l  partim d&ae;lm&ae;lum; furtum stalu  furtim stulorlice; uicissim stundm&ae;lum; strictim nearolice; affatim genihtsumlice sceort fa; praesertim huru &t;inga; paulatim lytlum; ET CETERA. 
 &D;as geendia&d; on um: dudum gefyrn  iterum eft  sursum upp  deorsum ny&d;er  desursum ufan  dedeorsum ny&t;an  deorsum uersum ny&d;erwerd  utroque uersum on &ae;g&d;re healfe werd  rursum and rursus eft  prorsum and prorsus eallunga  actutum hr&ae;dlice.

 On is geenda&d; satis genoh mann cwe&d; eac sat genoh butan is; satius bet; nimis &d;earle. 
 &T;as geendia&d; on sceortne us: haud secus na elles  caelitus heofonlice  stirpitus grundlunge o&d;&d;e mid stybbe mid ealle  funditus grundlunga  radicitus grundlunga o&d;&d;e mid wyrttruman mid ealle  mordicus hetelice o&t;&d;e bitm&ae;lum  actenus o&d; &d;is o&d;&d;e o&d; &t;&ae;t  diuinitus godcundlice  humanitus mennisclice man cwe&d; eac diuine and humane and humaniter m&ae;&d;lice  eminus foran ongean  cominus foran ongean  aduersus and aduersum ongean mid &t;wyrnysse aduersus is eac nama &t;wyr o&d;&d;e wi&d;err&ae;de. 
 On &d;issere geendunge ga&d; ealle COMPARATIVA: ocius hr&ae;dlicor  ac heora SVPERLATIVA geendia&d; on e: ocissime hr&ae;dlicost; diu lange  diutius leng  diutissime ealra lenggost; tarde late  tardius lator  tardissime latost: nuper niwan  nuperius niwlicor  nuperrime niwlicost; extra wi&d;utan  exterius wi&d;utan o&d;&d;e uttor  extreme swi&d;ost wi&d;utan; intra wi&d;innan  interius wi&d;innan o&d;&d;e innor  intime innemest; supra wi&d;ufan  superius ufor  supreme ufemest; infra wi&d;ny&t;an  inferius ny&d;or  infime ny&d;emest; crebro gelome  crebrius gelomlicor  creberrime gelomlicost; raro seldan  rarius seldor  rarissime ealra seldost. 
 Manega ga&d; on &t;as wisan. 
 potius swy&t;or and potissime swi&d;ost nabba&d; nanne POSITIVVM. 
 We ne magon &t;isne part fullice trahtnian on engliscum gereorde  ac we wylla&d; gyt hw&ae;t lytles be &t;am secgan. 
 immo gyt ma o&d;&d;e gyt swy&t;or by&d; on gecorennysse. 
 magis swy&t;or: magis hoc uolo  quam illud swy&d;or o&d;&d;e hra&d;or ic wylle &t;is  &t;onne &d;&ae;t. 
 quam bonus homo eala  hu god man. 
 tam bonus est iste eallswa god is &t;es. 
 uix earfo&d;lice: uix uoluit earfo&d;lice he wolde. 
 mox &t;ar rihte  deinceps sy&d;&d;an  dumtaxat &t;&ae;t an  tantummodo &t;&ae;t an; utrum uult hw&ae;&d;er he wylle; non uult he nele. 
 ADVERBIA beo&d; gelimplicor geendebyrde  gif hi standa&d; on foreweardan on &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce: bene agit wel he de&d;; sapienter loquitur wislice he sprec&d;. 
 Man mot hi eac b&ae;ftan settan butan &t;am  &d;e beo&d; anes st&ae;fgefeges o&d;&d;e &ae;teowigendlice o&d;&d;e astigendlice o&d;&d;e tihtendlice o&d;&d;e gelicnysse: &d;as sceolon &ae;fre standan on foreweardre spr&ae;ce. 
 o is toclypigendlic ADVERBIVM: o magister  doce me eala &d;u lareow  t&ae;c me. 
 He is eac wundrigendlic: o qualis facies eala hwylc ansyn. 
 He stent on foreweardan. 
 iam eallunga o&d;&d;e nu getacna&d; &t;reo tida: for&d;gewitene and andwerde and towearde  and stent on foreweardan. 
 dum ADVERBIVM getacna&d; for&d;gewitene tide and andwerde: ego legi  dum manducasti ic r&ae;dde  &d;a hwile &d;e &d;u &ae;te; lege  dum manduco r&ae;d  &d;a hwile &t;e ic ete. 
 He by&t; eac CONIVNCTIO. 
 intus sum ic eom wi&d;innan  foris sum ic eom ute  foras eo ut ic gange; eft uade foras gang ut. 
 de intus wi&d;innan  de foris wi&d;utan forbead DONATVS to cwe&d;enne  ac hi standa&d; swa &t;eah on halgum bocum. 
 DE PARTICIPIO. 
 PARTICIPIVM EST PARS ORATIONIS PARTEM CAPIENS NOMINIS PARTEMQVE VERBI. 
 &T;es part m&ae;g beon gehaten d&ae;lnimend  for&t;an &d;e he nim&d; of naman cynn and CASVS  and of worde he nim&d; tide and getacnunga: of him bam he nim&d; getel and gefegednysse. 
 PARTICIPIVM HABET SEX ACCIDENTIA d&ae;lnimend h&ae;f&d; syx gelimp: he h&ae;f&d; GENVS &t;&ae;t is cynn  CASVS gebigednys  TEMPVS tid  SIGNIFICATIO getacnunc  NVMERVS getel  FIGVRA gefegednys. 
 We wylla&d; nu secgan be &d;isum eallum gewislicor. 
 Ealle &d;a d&ae;lnimendan  &d;e getacnia&d; andwearde tide  syndon &d;reora cynna. 
 Of &d;am worde amo ic lufige cym&d; PARTICIPIVM andwerdre tide &t;reora cynna: hic et haec et hoc amans &t;es and &t;eos and &t;is lufiende  huius amantis and swa for&d; &ae;fter &t;&ae;re &d;riddan declinunge. 
 &D;a o&d;re ealle geendia&d; on us and synd MOBILIA  &t;&ae;t is awendendlice fram cynne to cynne: amatus gelufod to werlicum hade  amata to wiflicum cynne  amatum to na&d;rum cynne. 
 Eallswa doctus gel&ae;red he  docta heo  doctum hit. 
 &T;as &d;reo cynn synd on &d;ysum d&ae;le and na ma  for&d;an &d;e on &d;isum d&ae;le ne bi&d; nan COMMVNE DVVM GENERVM  &t;&ae;t is gem&ae;ne twegra cynna  ne nan EPICENON  &t;&ae;t is gemencged cynn. 
 Man cwe&d; on leden hic miluus &t;es glida  swa hw&ae;&d;er swa hit sy  he &t;e heo  and haec aquila &t;es earn  he and heo. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t gecynd nele ge&t;afian  &t;&ae;t &d;as cynn beon on &t;ysum d&ae;le. 
 Swaswa &d;a word belimpa&d; to &d;rym cynnum  swa eac &t;a PARTICIPIA  &d;e of &d;am wordum cuma&d;  belimpa&d; to &t;rym cynnum  to were and to wife and to na&d;rum cynne. 
 doceo ic t&ae;ce: wer t&ae;c&d; and wif t&ae;c&d; and MANCIPIVM  &t;&ae;t is weal  t&ae;c&d; sumne cr&ae;ft. 
 Nu cym&d; of &t;am worde PARTICIPIVM docens t&ae;cende &t;reora cynna and doctus gel&ae;red  docta  doctum  swaswa we &ae;r cw&ae;don. 
 Ealle  &t;a &t;e geendia&t; on us  folgia&d; &t;&ae;re o&d;re declinunge &ae;fter werlicum hade and  &t;a &d;e geendia&d; on um  ga&d; &ae;fter NEVTRVM and  &t;a &d;e geendia&d; on a  folgia&d; &t;&ae;re forman declinunge. 
 DE CASIBVS. 
 &D;es d&ae;l h&ae;f&d; six CASVS &ae;fre befullan  and heora nan ne ateora&d; on &ae;nigre declinunge  &t;eah &d;e sume naman don. 
 DE TEMPORIBVS. 
 &D;es d&ae;l h&ae;f&d; &t;a ylcan tida  &t;e &d;a word habba&d;  &t;e he of cym&d;. 
 &T;es part o&d;&d;e &t;es d&ae;l n&ae;f&d; nan angin ne n&ae;nne stede of him sylfum  ac by&d; of worde acenned and becym&d; sy&t;&t;an to his agenre ge&t;ing&d;e  swaswa nan o&d;er ne de&d;. 
 &D;a o&d;re seofan d&ae;las sindon sume frumcennede  sume cuma&d; of &d;am o&d;rum. 
 rex cyning is frumcenned nama  and regalis cynelic cym&d; of &t;am and h&ae;f&d; ealle &t;a &d;ing  &t;e his ealdor h&ae;f&d;; and ealswa ealle &t;a o&d;re d&ae;las. 
 Gif &d;onne se ofgangenda d&ae;l gewent to o&d;rum d&ae;le  &d;onne h&ae;f&d; he &d;a &d;ing eac  &d;e him to gebyria&d;. 
 bonus god is nama  and of &d;am cym&d; ADVERBIVM bene wel. 
 Nu h&ae;f&d; se bene &t;a &d;ing  &t;e ADVERBIO gebyra&d; to h&ae;bbenne  na &d;a &t;ing  &t;e naman gebyria&d;  &t;eah &d;e he of naman come. 
 Ealswa uigilo ic wacige is word  and of &d;am cym&d; nama uigil wacol  ac &t;&ae;t word h&ae;f&d; &t;a &d;ing  &t;e him to gebyria&d;  and se nama h&ae;f&d; &t;a &d;ing  &t;e him gebyria&d;  &t;onne he o&d;er d&ae;l is  o&d;er his ealdor; and swa gehwylce o&d;re. 
 Nu is PARTICIPIVM of worde and of worde cym&d;  by&d; swa &d;eah o&d;er d&ae;l and o&d;er &t;ing  o&d;er his ealdor bi&d;; and for &d;i h&ae;f&d; sume gelimp  &t;e his ealdor n&ae;f&d;  swylce he sy frumcenned  &d;eah &d;e he symle of o&d;rum cume. 
 Ne si nan man swa dysig  &t;&ae;t he &t;as gelicnysse to &ae;nigum halgum &t;inge awende  for&d;an &d;e &t;is is woruldcr&ae;ft fram u&d;witum aset to gesceadwisre spr&ae;ce and ne m&ae;g ne ne mot &ae;nigum halgum &t;inge beon geefenl&ae;ht. 
 PARTICIPIVM h&ae;f&d; &t;reo tida  praesens andwerd: legens r&ae;dende o&d;&d;e faciens wyrcende. 
 PRAETERITVM is for&d;gewiten: factus geworht. 
 FVTVRVM is towerd tid: facturus to wyrcenne. 
 Of d&ae;dlicum worde cuma&d; twegen PARTICIPIA. 
 An is andwerdre tide: legens r&ae;dende; o&d;er is towerdre tide: lecturus se &d;e r&ae;dan sceal; lecturus sum cras ic sceal r&ae;dan to merigen. 
 Of &d;am &t;rowiendlicum worde cuma&d; eft twegen PARTICIPIA: for&d;gewitenre tide  swaswa is lectus ger&ae;d; towerdre tide is legendus &t;&ae;t &d;e sceal beon ger&ae;d; and swa ungerime o&d;re. 
 Of na&d;res cynnes wordum cuma&d; eac PARTICIPIA andwerdre tide and towerdre tide  swaswa of d&ae;dlicum wordum: sto ic stande is NEVTRVM  and of &d;am is PARTICIPIVM stans standende and staturus se &d;e standan sceal. 
 Of &t;am fif &t;rowigendlicum neutrum cuma&d; &t;reo PARTICIPIA: gaudeo ic blissige  and of &d;am is gaudens blissigende and gauisus geblissod and gauisurus se &d;e blissian sceal; audeo ic dearr  audens gedyrstl&ae;cende  ausus dyrstig o&d;&d;e gedyrstl&ae;ht  ausurus se &d;e gedyrstl&ae;c&d;; soleo ic gewunige  solens wunigende  solitus gewunod to sumum &d;incge  soliturus se &d;e sceal beon gewunod; fio ic eom geworht o&d;&d;e geworden  fiens wur&t;ende  factus geworden o&d;&d;e geworht  fiendus &d;&ae;t &d;e gewur&d;an sceal; fido ic getruwige  fidens truwigende  fisus getruwod  fisurus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal truwian. 
 Of &d;am worde  &d;e is gecweden DEPONENS  cuma&d; &t;reo PARTICIPIA. 
 loquor ic sprece is DEPONENS  and of &d;am is PARTICIPIVM loquens sprecende and locutus se &d;e spr&ae;c and loquuturus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal sprecan. 
 On &t;am worde  &t;e is gecweden COMMVNE  cuma&d; feower PARTICIPIA  twegen d&ae;dlice and twegen &t;rowigendlice. 
 osculor ic cysse getacna&d; &ae;g&d;er ge d&ae;de ge &t;rowunge  and of &d;am is PARTICIPIVM osculans cyssende andwerdre tide  swaswa d&ae;dlice word. 
 O&d;er is for&d;gewitenre tide &t;rowigendlic: osculatus gecyssed. 
 Eac we cwe&d;a&d; osculatus sum ic cyste o&d;&d;e ic eom gecyssed  osculatus es to &t;am o&d;rum hade  osculatus est to &d;am &t;riddan hade. 
 Twegen sind towerde  an d&ae;dlic osculaturus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal cyssan and o&d;er &t;rowigendlic osculandus se &d;e sceal beon gecyssed. 
 Of eallum fulfremedum wordum cuma&d; PARTICIPIA  swaswa her awriten is  on fif wisan  and  &t;a &d;e sind andwerdre tide  &d;a sind &t;reora cynna. 
 Of &d;&ae;re forman CONIVGATIONE geendia&d; ealle on ans: amans lufigende  spirans or&d;igende; of &d;&ae;re o&d;re CONIVGATIONE geendia&d; on ens: docens t&ae;cende  habens h&ae;bbende; of &d;&ae;re &d;ryddan sume on ens  sume on iens: legens r&ae;dende  faciens wyrcende; of &d;&ae;re feor&d;an geendia&d; ealle on iens: audiens gehyrende  ueniens cumende. 
 Ealle &d;as word sind &t;reora cynna and ga&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;re &t;ryddan declinunge. 
 &D;a o&d;re geendia&d; sume on tus  sume on sus  sume on rus  sume on dus and wenda&d; heora FEMININVM on a and heora NEVTRVM on um  swaswa we &ae;r s&ae;don. 
 And &t;am casum hi beo&d; ge&d;eodde  &d;e &d;a word synd  &d;e hi of cuma&d;. 
 amo deum ic lufige god  amans deum lufigende god. 
 doceo pueros ic l&ae;re &t;a cild  docens pueros t&ae;cende &t;am cildum. 
 lego librum ic r&ae;de ane boc  legens librum r&ae;dende &t;a boc. 
 audio te ic gehyre &d;e  audiens te gehyrende &t;e. 
 &T;us ga&d; ealle m&ae;st d&ae;dlice word. 
 Sume nima&d; DATIVVM CASVM. 
 impero tibi ic bebeode &d;e and imperans tibi. 
 benedico tibi o&t;&d;e te ic bletsige &d;e  benedicens tibi o&d;&d;e te. 
 noceo tibi ic derige &d;e  nocens tibi. 
 inuideo tibi ic andige on &d;e  inuidens tibi. 
 parco tibi ic arige &d;e  parcens tibi. 
 respondeo tibi ic andswarige &d;e  respondens tibi. 
 &T;rowigendlice word beo&d; oftost ge&d;eodde ABLATIVVM: amor a te ic eom gelufod fram &d;e and PARTICIPIVM amatus a te gelufod fram &d;e; and swa fela o&d;re. 
 DEPONENTIA nyma&d; sume GENITIVVM and DATIVVM. 
 misereor tui and tibi and te ic miltsige &t;e  miserens tui and miserens illius miltsigende &d;in and miltsigende his. 
 We cwe&d;a&d; miserere nostri  domine and miserere nobis  domine miltsa us  drihten. 
 obliuiscor tui and tibi and te ic forgyte &d;e  obliuiscens tui and tibi and te. 
 recordor tui ic gemune &d;e o&d;&d;e ic eom &d;in gemyndig  recordans tui. 
 Sume ga&d; elles. 
 loquor uerbum ic sprece word and loquor ad te ic sprece to &d;e  loquens ad te o&d;&d;e loquutus  and loquor tibi. 
 precor deum ic bidde god  precans and precatus deum. 
 dignor te illa re ic gemedemige &d;e to &d;am &d;inge and dignans te illa re and medemigende &d;e to &d;am &d;inge. 
 careo mea pecunia ic &d;olige mines feos  carens sua re &d;oligende his &t;inges. 
 Ealle naman m&ae;st teo&d; GENITIVVM: amicus illius his freond  arator illius his yr&d;ling  faber regis &t;&ae;s cyninges smi&d;  reus mortis dea&d;es scyldig  ignarus doli nytende facn  securus armorum orsorh w&ae;pna. 
 Hi magon eac sume beon ge&d;eodde DATIVO gehiwodlice: amicus illi est he is him freond  scriptor illi est he is him writere  &t;&ae;t is &d;am men  &t;e he writ. 
 Sume nima&d; ACCVSSATIVVM gehiwodlice: exosus bella onscuniende gefeoht  praescius futura forewitig toweardra &d;inga. 
 Sume teo&d; ABLATIVVM: dignus est bono he is wyr&d;e godes  dignus est morte he is wyr&d;e dea&d;es  mactus uirtute ge&t;ogen on m&ae;gne. 
 And eallswa hi ga&d; menigfealdlice and to &ae;lcum cynne. 
 &D;&ae;t word  &t;e we cwe&d;a&d; sum ic eom  es &t;u eart  est he is; ET PLVRALITER sumus we sind  estis ge synd  sunt hi synd of &t;issum worde cw&ae;don &t;a ealdan boceras PARTICIPIVM andwerdre tide ens  ac hit nis nu na gewunelic. 
 Of &d;am is swa &d;eah gefeged potens mihtig. 
 Of &d;am worde cym&d; PRAETERITVM fui ic w&ae;s  and his toweardra PARTICIPIVM is futurus  &d;&ae;t we cwe&d;a&d; &ae;fre towerd. 
 &T;&ae;t word eo ic fare is &d;u f&ae;rst  it he f&ae;r&d; maca&d; PARTICIPIVM iens farende  euntis farendes. 
 Eallswa of queo ic m&ae;g quiens magende  queuntis queunti and swa for&d;  and ealle  &t;a &d;e of him gefegede beo&d;  habba&d; e and u on &d;am fif gebigedum casum. 
 Heora toweardan PARTICIPIA synd &d;as: iturus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal faran; quiturus  ac we ne cunnon nan englisc &t;&ae;r to. 
 Sume ga&d; of &t;am regole  for&d;an &d;e se gewuna is strengra. 
 eruo ic generie  erutus generod: nu wolde se regol &t;&ae;s cr&ae;ftes habban of &d;am eruturus  ac se gewuna hylt eruiturus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal nerian orior ic up aspringe  ortus up asprungen  oriturus se &d;e wyle o&d;&d;e sceal up aspringan. 
 pario ic cenne &t;is gebyra&d; to wimmannum  partus acenned  pariturus se &d;e cennan sceal. 
 fruor ic bruce  fructus gebrocen  fruiturus se &d;e brucan sceal. 
 fungor ic bruce maca&d; functus gebrocen and functurus se &d;e brucan sceal; of &d;am bi&d; defunctus for&d;faren  se &d;e his timan breac. 
 Gyf &t;a word ateoria&d;  &t;onne ateoria&d; eac &t;a PARTICIPIA  &d;e him of cuman sceoldon. 
 DE NVMERO. 
 NVMERVS is getel: on &d;isum d&ae;le SINGVLARIS anfeald currens yrnende ET PLVRALIS and menigfeald currentes yrnende; and hi n&ae;fre ne ateoria&d; on na&d;rum getele &t;e ma  &t;e on casum. 
 DE FIGVRA. 
 Ne bi&d; nan PARTICIPIVM gefeged  buton &t;&ae;t word  &t;e he of cym&d;  beo &ae;r gefeged. 
 facio ic wyrce is anfeald word  and of &d;am is anfeald PARTICIPIVM faciens wyrcende. 
 Of &d;am is gefeged perficio ic gefremme  and of &d;am is gefeged PARTICIPIVM perficiens gefremmende; and swa fela o&d;re. 
 Gif &d;onne se PARTICIPIVM bi&d; gefeged &t;urh hine sylfne and &t;&ae;t word ne bi&d; na gefeged  &t;onne wyr&d; se PARTICIPIVM to naman. 
 noceo ic derige and of &t;am nocens deriende &ae;g&d;er ge PARTICIPIVM ge nama: innocens unsce&d;&d;ig is &ae;fre nama  for&d;an &d;e he is gefeged buton &t;am worde: innoceo ne bi&d; na gewunelic word. 
 sapio ic wat  and of &d;am sapiens wis is PARTICIPIVM and nama: insipiens unwis o&d;&d;e unsnotor is &ae;fre nama  for&d;an &d;e he is swa gefeged  swa &t;&ae;t word ne m&ae;g beon  &t;e he of com; and swa fela o&d;re. 
 Eft  gif hi beo&d; wi&d;metene  &t;&ae;t is  gif hi beo&d; COMPARATIVA  &d;onne beo&d; hi eac naman. 
 indulgens miltsigende  indulgentior mildre; acceptus andfencge  acceptior andfengra; and fela o&d;re. 
 Sume synd &ae;g&d;er ge PARTICIPIA ge naman. 
 passus ge&t;rowod is PARTICIPIVM of &d;am worde patior ic &t;rowige  and eft passus st&ae;pe is nama. 
 lapsus asliden of &t;am worde labor ic &ae;tslide  and lapsus slide is nama. 
 monitus gemyngod of &t;am worde moneo ic mynegige  and monitus mynegung is nama; and swa gehwylce o&d;re. 
 Ac  gif hi beo&d; PARTICIPIA  &t;onne beo&d; hi &d;&ae;re o&d;re declinunge and MOBILIA. 
 Gif hi beo&d; naman  &t;onne beo&d; hi &d;&ae;re feor&d;an declinunge and FIXA  &t;&ae;t is unawendendlice. 
 Eallswa eft uisus gesewen is PARTICIPIVM  and uisus gesih&d; is nama. 
 auditus gehyrd is PARTICIPIVM  and auditus hlist is nama. 
 ictus gecnysed and ictus sweng o&d;&d;e cnyssung. 
 tactus gehrepod and tactus hrepung. 
 habitus geh&ae;fd and habitus gyrla. 
 usus gebrocen and usus bryce and o&d;re &t;yllice. 
 Eft natus acenned is PARTICIPIVM  and meus natus min bearn is nama o&d;&d;e natus illius his sunu. 
 Eft amans deum lufigende god is PARTICIPIVM  and amans dei is nama  &t;&ae;t is amator dei  godes lufigend; and amans uirtutis mihte lufigend. 
 factum geworht PARTICIPIVM and factum d&ae;d. 
 dictum gecweden and dictum cwyde. 
 audiendus se &d;e sceal beon gehyred and audiendus est he is to gehyrenne nama. 
 habendus se &d;e sceal beon geh&ae;fd and habendus est he is to h&ae;bbenne. 
 scriptura is FEMININVM PARTICIPIVM of scripturus  and scriptura is gewrit nama. 
 Ealswa pictura seo &d;e metan sceal and pictura meting. 
 statura seo &d;e standan sceal and statura mannes leng. 
 usura seo &d;e brucan sceal and usura gafol. 
 litura seo &d;e cl&ae;man sceal and litura cl&ae;ming. 
 diligentia is menigfeald NEVTRVM of diligens  and haec diligentia &t;eos geornfulnys is nama. 
 abstinentia is menigfeald PARTICIPIVM and abstinentia forh&ae;fednys. 
 Ealswa sapientia PARTICIPIVM and wisdom; and swa fela o&d;re. 
 Sume beo&d; &ae;fre naman  for&d;an &d;e hi ne cuma&d; na of wordum: capillatus sidfexede; comatus se &d;e loccas h&ae;f&d;: coma is loc; auris is eare  and of &d;am is auritus se &d;e h&ae;f&d; mycele earan. 
 nasus nosu  nasatus se &d;e h&ae;f&d; mycele nosu; dens to&d;  dentatus se &d;e h&ae;f&d; mycele te&d;; barba beard  barbatus gebyrd; galea helm  galeatus gehelmod; lorica byrne  loricatus gebyrnod; scutum scyld  scutatus gescyldod. 
 gladius swurd  gladiatus geswurdod; asta sceaft o&d;&d;e spere  astatus gesperod; purpura purpur  purpuratus mid purpuran gescryd; pallium p&ae;l  palliatus mid p&ae;lle gescryd; tonica tunece  tonicatus mid tunecan gescryd; arma w&ae;pnu  armatus gew&ae;pnod. 
 gemma gimstan  gemmatus gegymmod; littera st&ae;f  litteratus se &d;e can st&ae;fcr&ae;ft; cornu horn  cornutus gehyrned; astu pr&ae;t  astutus p&ae;tig. 
 &D;as and &t;yllice sindon MOBILIA NOMINA  &d;&ae;t is awendendlice naman  for&d;an &t;e hi nabba&d; word on gewunan  buton armatus is &ae;g&d;er ge nama ge PARTICIPIVM: armo ic w&ae;pnige sumne man is d&ae;dlic word  and armor ic eom gew&ae;pnod is &d;rowigendlic  and of &d;am is armatus  &t;onne hit bi&d; PARTICIPIVM and tide getacna&d;. 
 DE CONIVNCTIONE. 
 CONIVNCTIO EST PARS ORATIONIS INDECLINABILIS ADNECTENS ORDINANSQVE SENTENTIAM. 
 CONIVNCTIO m&ae;g beon gecweden ge&t;eodnys. 
 Se is an d&ae;l ledenspr&ae;ce undeclinigendlic gef&ae;stniende and endebyrdigende &ae;lcne cwyde. 
 Swaswa lim gef&ae;stna&d; fel to sumum brede  swa getig&d; seo CONIVNCTIO &t;a word tog&ae;dere. 
 &T;es d&ae;l gef&ae;stna&d; and gefr&ae;twa&d; ledenspr&ae;ce and hwilon tosc&ae;t and hwilon geendebyrt. 
 pius et fortis fuit Dauid rex arf&ae;st and strang w&ae;s DAVID cyning: se et is CONIVNCTIO  &t;&ae;t is on englisc and. 
 ego et tu ic and &d;u  nos et uos we and ge wylla&d; an. 
 Nu &t;u miht gehyran  hu &t;es d&ae;l tig&d; &t;a word tog&ae;dere. 
 N&ae;f&d; &t;es d&ae;l nane mihte ne nan andgit  gif he ana stent  ac on endebyrdnysse ledenspr&ae;ce he gelima&d; &t;a word  ne he ne bi&d; naht on englisc awend butan o&d;rum wordum. 
 TRIA ACCIDVNT CONIVNCTIONI &t;reo &d;ing gelimpa&d; &t;isum d&ae;le: an is POTESTAS miht  o&d;er is FIGVRA gefegednys  &t;ridda ORDO endebyrdnys. 
 POTESTAS is miht  and seo geswutela&d;  hw&ae;t &t;es d&ae;l m&ae;ge fremman  for&d;an &d;e he hwilon ge&t;eot o&d;re d&ae;las and hwilon tosc&ae;t. 
 Sume sindon gehatene COPVLATIVAE  &t;&ae;t sind ge&d;eodendlice  for&d;an &d;e hi ge&d;eoda&d; o&d;re d&ae;las on &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce endebyrdnysse  ac hi nabba&d; nan andgit  gif hi ana standa&d;. 
 &T;as sind ge&t;eodendlice: et  que  ac ast  at  atque. 
 uir et mulier wer and wif. 
 stetitque and he stod. 
 cantauitque and he sang. 
 omnis populus uirorum ac mulierum eall folc wera and wifa. 
 ast alii adfirmant and o&d;re se&t;a&d;. 
 at is ongeanweardlic: at Iesus ait and se h&ae;lend cw&ae;&d; him togeanes; at illi tacuerunt and hi suwodon togeanes &t;&ae;s h&ae;lendes wordum. 
 atque aliis est largus and o&t;rum he is cystig. 
 Ealle &d;as habba&d; an englisc  &t;eah &d;e hi for f&ae;gernysse fela synd on ledenspr&ae;ce. 
 Sume synd gehatene DISIVNCTIVAE  &t;&ae;t synd ascyrigendlice  for&d;an &d;e hi totw&ae;ma&d; &t;&ae;t andgyt and &t;a word ge&d;eoda&d;. 
 Her synd &d;a: aut  ue  uel  ne nec  an  neque. 
 lege aut scribe r&ae;d o&d;&d;e writ. 
 aut aliquis latet error o&d;&d;e sum gedwyld luta&d; &t;&ae;r. 
 ne lingua nec manus oculiue peccent ne tunge ne handa o&d;&d;e eagan syngion. 
 sentisne? understentst &t;u la? 
 uisne? wylt &t;u la? 
 uel dies est o&d;&d;e nox o&d;&d;e hit is d&ae;g o&d;&d;e niht. 
 tota die o&d;&d;e legit iste o&d;&t;e cogitat eallne d&ae;g o&d;&d;e &t;es man r&ae;t o&d;&d;e he &t;enc&d;. 
 nec laudo nec uitupero ne ic ne herige ne ic ne t&ae;le.

 Her synd &d;a: autem  enim  uero  quidem  equidem  quoque  nam  namque  uidelicet.

 Sume sindon CAVSALES gehatene.

 etiamsi mortuus fuerit  uiuet &t;eah &d;e he beo dead  he leofa&d;. 
 DONATVS tel&d; gyt ma to &d;isum: ni  nisi  sed.

 RATIO is gescead  and &t;as sind for sumon gesceade gesette on endebyrdnysse ledenspr&ae;ce: ergo  igitur  ita  itaque  utique.

 PRISCIANVS cw&ae;&d;  &t;&ae;t sume sind ADVERSATIVAE  &t;&ae;t sind wi&t;err&ae;dlice.

 Se o&d;er licet n&ae;f&d; naht &d;yses.

 DE FIGVRA. 
 Feawa CONIVNCTIONES beo&d; gefegede. 
 si and que and ne underfo&d; feginge &d;us: si quis swa hwa  si quando gif &ae;fre o&d;&t;e ahw&ae;nne; ne quis: ne quis furetur &t;&ae;t nan ne stele  ne quando obdormiam in morte &t;&ae;t ic n&ae;fre on dea&d;e ne slape; and &t;as sind MOBILIA. 
 quisque gehwa  ubique gehw&ae;r  undique &ae;ghwanon. 
 On &t;isum &ae;ftemystan nis na se que ENCLETICA  for&d;an &d;e he ne ahylt &d;one sweg him to. 
 Swaswa his gewuna is.

 DE ORDINE. 
 ORDO is endebyrdnys  and sume CONIVNCTIONES &ae;fter gecynde standa&d; &ae;fre on foreweardan on &ae;lcere ledenspr&ae;ce  swaswa do&d; &t;as: at  ast  si and gehwylce o&d;re.

 INCIPIT PRAEPOSITIO. 
 PRAEPOSITIO EST PARS ORATIONIS INDECLINABILIS. 
 PRAEPOSITIO m&ae;g beon gecweden on englisc foresetnys  for&d;an &d;e he stent &ae;fre on foreweardan  swa hw&ae;r swa he by&d;  beo he gefeged to o&d;rum worde  ne beo he. 
 Hwilon he geeacna&d; and gefyl&d; &t;&ae;ra worda andgit  &d;e he to cym&d;  and hwilon he awent heora getacnunge and hwilon wana&d;. 
 celsus is healic. 
 Do &d;&ae;r to PRAEPOSITIO ex  &t;onne by&d; hit excelsus swy&d;e healic: her he gefyl&d; &t;&ae;t andgit. 
 iustus is rihtwis. 
 Do &d;&ae;r to PRAEPOSITIO in  &t;onne by&d; hit iniustus unrihtwis: her he awent &t;&ae;t andgit. 
 rideo ic hliche. 
 Do &d;&ae;r to PRAEPOSITIO sub  &t;onne by&d; hit subrideo ic smercige: her he gewana&d; &t;&ae;t andgit and swa gehw&ae;r. 
 An &t;ing gelimp&d; &t;isum d&ae;le  &t;&ae;t is CASVS. 
 Twegen CASVS he tyh&d; him to  ACCVSATIVVM and ABLATIVVM. 
 We wylla&d; nu &ae;rest awritan &t;a PRAEPOSITIONES  &t;e belimpa&d; to ACCVSSATIVVM  ac hi nabba&d; na full andgyt  gyf hi ana standa&d; butan o&d;rum wordum. 
 Her synd &d;a: ad  apud  ante  aduersum  cis  citra  circum  circa  contra  erga  extra  inter  intra  infra  iuxta  ob  pone  per  prope  propter  secundum  post  trans  ultra  praeter  supra  circiter  usque  secus  penes.

 trans uadum ofer &t;one ford  trans mare ofer s&ae;. 
 ultra mare est begeondan s&ae; he is  ultra te begeondan &d;e. 
 praeter illa toforan &d;am o&d;&d;e butan &t;am; eft spem in alium numquam habui  praeter in te  deus Israel n&ae;fde ic n&ae;nne hiht on o&d;erne n&ae;fre  buton on &d;e  Israhela god. 
 supra pectus domini bufan drihtnes breoste. 
 circiter tria milia fornean &t;reo &t;usend  circiter triginta annos fornean &t;rittig geara  circiter kalendas wi&d; &d;am mon&d;e kalendae synd clypunga  for&d;an &d;e &d;a ealdan men clypodon symle on niwum monan. 
 usque nim&d; oftost o&d;erne PRAEPOSITIO him to: usque ad faeces biberunt hi druncon o&d; &d;a drosna  usque ad uesperum o&d; &ae;fen. 
 secus uiam wi&d; &t;one weg  secus uadum sedet wi&d; &d;one ford he sit. 
 penes uos est mid eow he is  penes iudices mid demum. 
 &T;as PRAEPOSITIONES sume magon beon ADVERBIA  gif hi beo&d; b&ae;ftan gesette.

 &D;as o&d;re beo&d; ge&d;eodde to ABLATIVVM: a  ab  abs  cum  coram  clam  de  e  ex  pro  prae  palam  sine  absque  tenus. 
 We cwe&d;a&d; on ledenspr&ae;ce a domo of huse o&d;&d;e fram huse. 
 ab homine fram men  ab illo fram him. 
 abs quolibet iussu butan &ae;nigre h&ae;se. 
 cum exercitu pergit mid here he f&ae;r&d;. 
 cum rege est mid cynincge he is. 
 coram uobis stat &ae;tforan eow he stent. 
 clam is swi&d;or ADVERBIVM  &t;onne PRAEPOSITIO: bona aperte facit  mala clam god he de&d; openlice and yfel digellice; her is clam ADVERBIVM  ac he bi&d; swa &t;eah PRAEPOSITIO  &t;onne he bi&d; foreset: clam custodibus surgo nytendum &d;am weardmannum ic arise  clam te est digele &d;e is. 
 de loco fram stowe o&d;&d;e be stowe  de domo dei of godes huse  de illo homine loquor be &d;am men ic sprece  de rege loquitur episcopus be &d;am cyncge sprec&d; se bisceop. 
 e terra of eor&d;an  fons ascendebat e terra se wyll astah up of &d;&ae;re eor&d;an. 
 ex illo loco of &d;&ae;re stowe. 
 pro hominibus oro for mannum ic gebidde. 
 prae timore non audeo for ege ic ne dear. 
 palam omnibus dico openlice ic secge him eallum. 
 sine labore hic sedeo butan geswince ic sitte her  sine crimine butan leahtre. 
 absque terrore quiescit butan ogan he hine gerest  absque ambiguitate butan twynunge. 
 tenus is ADVERBIVM mid Grecum  ac he is mid Ledenwarum geteald to PRAEPOSITIO  for&d;an &d;e he ne m&ae;g an standende &ae;nige mihte habban  and by&d; oftost swa &d;eah geendebyrd b&ae;ftan: capulotenus abdidit ensem o&d; &d;a hylta he behydde &t;&ae;t swurd.

 obsto ic ongean stande  obuius ongean cumende.

 INCIPIT INTERIECTIO. 
 Interiectio est pars orationis significans mentis affectum uoce incondita  interiectio is an d&ae;l ledenspr&ae;ce getacnjende &t;&ae;s modes gewilnunge mid ungesceapenre stemne.

 XXV sume sind gehatene SCEMATA  &t;&ae;t sind mislice hiw and f&ae;gernyssa on ledenspr&ae;ce  hu heo betst gelogod beo. 
 XXVI sume sind gehatene TROPI  &t;&ae;t sind mislice getacnunga o&d;&d;e wisan on ledenspr&ae;ce abrodene of heora agenre getacnunge to o&d;re gelicnysse  swaswa is gecweden fluctuare segetes  gemmare uites  &t;&ae;t &ae;ceras y&d;ia&d; and wintreowa gimmia&d;  for&d;an &d;e &ae;ceras fara&d; on sumera  swaswa s&ae; y&d;igende  and wintreowa blostman beo&d; gimmum gelice. 
 Ealswa floridam iuuentutem et lacteam caniciem &d;a blostmb&ae;ran iugu&d;e and &t;a meolchwitan harunge. 
 XXVII sum &d;&ae;ra is PROSA  &t;&ae;t is for&d;riht leden buton leo&d;cr&ae;fte gelencged and gelogod. 
 XXVIII sume sind gehatene METRA on grecisc  &d;&ae;t is on leden MENSVRAE and on englisc gemetu. 
 &D;a gemetu gebyria&d; to ledenum leo&d;cr&ae;fte. 
 Se cr&ae;ft is swa ameten  &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;r ne mot beon fur&d;on an st&ae;f ofer getel  ac beo&d; ealle &t;a fers geemnytte be anum getele  gif hit aht beon sceal. 
 XXIX sume synd gehatene FABVLAE  &t;&ae;t synd idele spellunga. 
 FABVLAE synd &t;a saga  &t;e menn secga&d; ongean gecynde  &t;&ae;t &d;e n&ae;fre ne gewear&d; ne gewur&d;an ne m&ae;g. 
 XXX sum &d;&ae;ra is gehaten HISTORIA  &t;&ae;t is gerecednyss. 
 Mid &t;&ae;re man awrit and gereh&d; &t;a &d;ing and &t;a d&ae;da  &t;e w&ae;ron gedone on ealdum dagum and us dyrne w&ae;ron. 
 SY &t;EOS BOC &d;VS HER GEENDOD. 
 On ledenspr&ae;ce synd menigfealde getel  ac on englisc nis nan &d;&ae;ra gewunelic butan &t;rim anum. 
 libra on leden is pund on englisc. 
 Fif penegas gemacia&d; &ae;nne scylling and &t;rittig penega &ae;nne mancus.
